NID 6 is 'PalanquinDark-Regular', Everything looks good.

Palanquin Dark Medium Regular (PalanquinDark-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'PalanquinDark-Medium', Everything looks good.

Pass

Palanquin Dark Medium Regular (PalanquinDark-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Palanquin Dark' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Palanquin Dark Medium'.

Pass

Palanquin Dark SemiBold Regular (PalanquinDark-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'PalanquinDark-SemiBold', Everything looks good.

Palanquin Dark SemiBold Regular (PalanquinDark-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Palanquin Dark' + 'Space' + NID 17 'SemiBold' = NID 1 'Palanquin Dark SemiBold'.

PostScript names

Postscript names should not be longer then 29 characters. May cause issues in PDF.

Is longer:
'dv_MatraShortERephCandraBindu
dv_MatraCandraORephCandraBindu

dv_MatraCandraERephCandraBindu'
